 - input bhashaa se Ekadashi of Bhadrapada Krishna Paksha is known as Aja Ekadashi
 is din vrath rakhkar bhagwaan vishnu kii puja karne se saare kashton se mukti milti he
 According to the scriptures, on this day, King Harishchandra got his lost family and kingdom back on this fast
 kehete hai jis kaamana se koi yah vrath karata he, uski vah sabhi manokamanaayen tatkaal hi puri ho jaati hai
 During this fast, Lord Vishnu is worshiped in the form of Upendra
 pandit vinod mishra ke anusaar is baar anndaa evam aja ekadshi kaa vrath 18 agast ko he or isi din vatsa dwadashi bhi he tathaa bhagwaan ko priy gaay or bachhadon kaa pujan karnaa chahie tathaa unhen gud or ghaas bhi khilaani chahie
 How to worship and fast
 
 
 -aja ekadshi vratako jo vyakti is vrath ko rakhana chaahate hai unhen dashami tithi ko satvik bhojan karnaa chahie taaki vrath ke dauraan man shuddh rahe
 On the day of Ekadashi, in the morning at sunrise, after bathing, one should worship Lord Vishnu by lighting a lamp of ghee, worshiping it with fruits and flowers
 - bhagwaan kii puja ke baad vishnu sahasranam yaa phir gita kaa paath karnaa chahie
 - There is a law for fasting to remain unharmed and waterless during the day, but the scripture also says that sick and children can make fruit
 - saamaanya sthiti main raatri main bhagwaan kii puja ke baad jal or fal grahan karnaa chahie
 Night awakening has great significance in this fast
 - dwadashi tithi ke din praatah brahman ko bhojan karwaane ke baad swayan bhojan karnaa chahie
 Keep in mind that do not eat brinjal on Dwadashi
 kya he vrath kathasatyuga main suryavanshi chakravarti raja harishchandra hue jo bade satyawadee the
 Once, for the sake of his promise, he donated his entire kingdom to Rajvishi Vishwamitra
 dakshina dene ke liye apni patni evam putr ko hi nahin swayan tak ko das ke rup main ek chandal ko bech daalaa
 Despite suffering many troubles, he was not distracted from the truth, then one day he met Rishi Gautama, who told him to observe this fast while reciting the glory of Aja Ekadashi
 raja harishchandr ne apni samarthyanusaar is vrath ko kiya, jiske prabhaav se unhen na keval unka khoyaa hua rajya praapt hua, balki parivaar sahit sabhi prakaar ke sukh bhogate hue ant main vah prabhu ke paramdhaam ko praapt hue
 All their sins were destroyed and they lost their lost kingdom and family also due to the effect of fasting of Aaja Ekadashi
 aja ekadshi kaa falpuraanon main bataaya gaya he ki jo vyakti shrriddha purvak aja ekadshi kaa vrath rakhata he uske purv janm ke paap cat jate hai or is janm main sukh-samruddhi kii prapti hoti he
 Fasting of Aja Ekadashi leads to the attainment of virtue similar to performing the Ashwamedha Yajna and after death one attains a place in the best world
